Xim Sansにおいて私用領域などに存在しているUnicode未登録文字をUnicode公式っぽく紹介します。
いくつか「にしき的フォント」や「Quivira」などの他フォントに含まれている文字もあるため、参考としてそちらも参照しております。

なお、これらの文字を入力する時は日本語入力モードなら「Unicode値＋F5キー」でUnicode値から文字を入力できるので便利。

#	Latin Extensions
##	Latin extensions for Koalib
	U+E000
　LATIN  CAPITAL LETTER AT
　　https://unicode.org/L2/L2019/19006-capital-at.pdf
　　•used for Koalib
　　•F248 in nishiki-teki font
　　•F004 in Quivira
	U+E001
　LATIN  SMALL LETTER AT
　　https://unicode.org/L2/L2019/19006-capital-at.pdf
　　•used for Koalib
　　•F247 in nishiki-teki font
　　•F005 in Quivira

　LATIN CAPITAL LETTER REVERSED SCRUPLE
　　www.pentzlin.com/EPA_Proposal_Draft1.pdf
　　http://std.dkuug.dk/jtc1/sc2/wg2/docs/n4079.pdf
　　https://unicode.org/L2/L2011/11040-epa-proposal.pdf
　　https://www.unicode.org/L2/L2023/23074-slovene-metelko.pdf
　　= latin capital letter rounded e
　　•lowercase for EPA is E00F  latin small letter c with palatal hook
　　•lowercase for SMA is E0B4  latin small letter reversed scruple
　　•the serif on the middle bar is sometimes retained or modified in sans-serif fonts
　　•denotes the sound [tʃ] in the English Phonotypic Alphabet
　　•denotes the sound [e] in the Slovene Metelko alphabet
　　→ 0404 Є cyrillic capital letter ukrainian ie
　　→ 2108 ℈ scruple
　　→ A792 Ꞓ latin capital letter c with bar

　　http://www.unicode.org/L2/L2017/17311-n4848-lute.pdf
　　•indicates that the string is to be plucked outwards
　　•on the right of a tablature symbol in vertical layout, or above in horizontal layout
◌	U+EC3D
　CHINESE LUTE COMBINING LEADING DOT
　　http://www.unicode.org/L2/L2017/17311-n4848-lute.pdf
　　•indicates that the string is to be plucked with the index finger
　　•above a tablature symbol in vertical layout, or on the left in horizontal layout
◌	U+EC3E
　CHINESE LUTE COMBINING TRAILING DOT
　　http://www.unicode.org/L2/L2017/17311-n4848-lute.pdf
　　•indicates that the string is to be plucked with the thumb
　　•beneath a tablature symbol in vertical layout, or on the right in horizontal layout
◌	U+EC3F
　CHINESE LUTE CHORD MARK
　　http://www.unicode.org/L2/L2017/17311-n4848-lute.pdf
　　•appended to the last character in a sequence of two to four tabalature symbols
representing a chord
　　•positioned on the right of a sequence of tabalature symbols in vertical layout, or above the sequence in horizontal layout

#	Latin Extensions
##	Slovene Metelko alphabets
	U+F3E9

　　https://www.unicode.org/L2/L2023/23074-slovene-metelko.pdf
	U+F3EA
　LATIN SMALL LETTER H WITH NOTCH
　　https://www.unicode.org/L2/L2023/23074-slovene-metelko.pdf
	U+F3EB
　LATIN CAPITAL LETTER L WITH PIGTAIL AT BOTTOM
　　https://www.unicode.org/L2/L2023/23074-slovene-metelko.pdf
　　•resembles the digraph "Lj" in modern Slovene orthography
　　→ 027A ɺ latin small letter turned r with long leg
	U+F3EC
　LATIN CAPITAL LETTER N WITH INWARDS HOOK
　　https://www.unicode.org/L2/L2023/23074-slovene-metelko.pdf
　　•resembles the digraph "Nj" in modern Slovene orthography
	U+F3ED
　LATIN SMALL LETTER N WITH INWARDS HOOK
　　https://www.unicode.org/L2/L2023/23074-slovene-metelko.pdf
　　https://unicode.org/L2/L2011/11135-lithuanian.pdf
　　•also used in modern Lithuanian dialectology
	U+F3EE

　　https://www.unicode.org/L2/L2023/23074-slovene-metelko.pdf
　　→ 0429 Щ cyrillic capital letter shcha

　　= light

　　→ 2260 ≠ not equal to

##	Combining Marks
	U+F7FE
　WASEDA SHORTHAND COMBINING REPETITION DOT
　　•repeats the previous one or two syllables
　　→ 309D ゝ hiragana iteration mark
	U+F7FF
　WASEDA SHORTHAND COMBINING REPETITION OVERLINE
　　•repeats the previous three or more syllables
　　→ 3031 〱 vertical kana repeat mark
